1 External loop back

00 Normal signal path (default).
01 RAM Test Mode: Internal busses are multiplexed to make all RAM blocks of the 32-bit SCU module directly accessible by the Host. This mode is intended to enable testing of the embedded RAM blocks during production testing.
10 I/O Test Mode: Output pins are driven to the values defined by bits TXA, TXB, TXENA, TXENB. The values applied to the input pins can be read from register bits RXA and RXB.

The error codes regarding CAS / MTS symbols concern only the monitored bit pattern, irrelevant whether those bit patterns are seen in the symbol window or elsewhere.

ERAY_SUCC1

"SUC Configuration Register 1"

AddressERAY_SUCC1_ADDR = 0xF0010080
Absolute addressableNo
Reset value0x0C401080
C typeERAY_SUCC1_t

ERAY_SUCC1.bits "SUC Configuration Register 1"
Mask:ERAY_SUCC1_MASK = 0x0ffffb8f
Masks:  ERAY_SUCC1_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:ERAY_SUCC1_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
CMD 4 0 - 3 rwh 0x0000000f CHI Command Vector
0000 COMMAND_NOT_ACCEPTED"
0001 CONFIG
0010 READY
0011 WAKEUP
0100 RUN
0101 ALL_SLOTS
0110 HALT
0111 FREEZE
1000 SEND_MTS
1001 ALLOW_COLDSTART
1010 RESET_STATUS_INDICATORS
1011 MONITOR_MODE
1100 CLEAR_RAMS
1101 Reserved
1110 Reserved
1111 Reserved
PBSY 1 7 - 7 rh 0x00000080 POC Busy
0 POC not busy, SUCC1.CMD writeable
1 POC is busy, SUCC1.CMD locked
TXST 1 8 - 8 rw 0x00000100 Transmit Startup Frame in Key SlotThis bit can be updated in "DEFAULT_CONFIG" or "CONFIG" state only!The protocol requires that both bits TXST and TXSY are set for coldstart nodes. (pKeySlotUsedForStartup)
0 No Startup Frame transmission in key slot, node is non-coldstarter
1 Key slot used to transmit startup Frame, node is leading or following coldstarter
TXSY 1 9 - 9 rw 0x00000200 Transmit SYNC Frame in Key Slot(pKeySlotUsedForSync)
0 No SYNC Frame transmission in key slot, node is neither sync nor coldstart node
1 Key slot used to transmit SYNC Frames, node is sync node
CSA 5 11 - 15 rw 0x0000f800 Cold Start Attempts(gColdStartAttempts)
PTA 5 16 - 20 rw 0x001f0000 Passive to Active (pAllowPassiveToActive)
WUCS 1 21 - 21 rw 0x00200000 Wakeup Channel Select (pWakeupChannel)
0 Send wakeup pattern on channel A
1 Send wakeup pattern on channel B
TSM 1 22 - 22 rw 0x00400000 Transmission Slot Mode (pSingleSlotEnabled)
0 ALL Slot Mode
1 SINGLE Slot Mode (default after application reset)
HCSE 1 23 - 23 rw 0x00800000 Halt due to Clock Sync Error (pAllowHaltDueToClock)
0 Communication Controller will enter / remain in "NORMAL_PASSIVE"
1 Communication Controller will enter "HALT" state
MTSA 1 24 - 24 rw 0x01000000 Select Channel A for MTS TransmissionMTSA and MTSB may also be changed outside "DEFAULT_CONFIG" or "CONFIG" state when the write to SUCC1 register is directly preceded by the unlock sequence as described in Lock Register (LCK). This may be combined with CHI command "SEND_MTS". If both bits MTSA and MTSB are set to 1 an MTS symbol will be transmitted on both channels when requested by writing SUCC1.CMD = 1000B.
0 Channel A disabled for MTS transmission
1 Channel A selected for MTS transmission
MTSB 1 25 - 25 rw 0x02000000 Select Channel B for MTS Transmission
0 Channel B disabled for MTS transmission
1 Channel B selected for MTS transmission
CCHA 1 26 - 26 rw 0x04000000 Connected to Channel A (pChannels)
0 Not connected to channel A
1 Node connected to channel A (default after application reset)
CCHB 1 27 - 27 rw 0x08000000 Connected to Channel B (pChannels)
0 Not connected to channel B
1 Node connected to channel B (default after application reset)
 readable0x0ffffb8f 
writeable0x0ffffb0f
volatile0x0000008f

1 Cold starting of node disabled
WSV 3 16 - 18 rh 0x00070000 Wakeup Status (vPOC!WakeupStatus)
000 UNDEFINED. Wakeup not yet executed by the Communication Controller.
001 RECEIVED_HEADER. Set when the Communication Controller finishes wakeup due to the reception of a Frame Header without coding violation on either channel in "WAKEUP_LISTEN" state.
010 RECEIVED_WUP. Set when the Communication Controller finishes wakeup due to the reception of a valid wakeup pattern on the configured wakeup channel in "WAKEUP_LISTEN" state.
011 COLLISION_HEADER. Set when the Communication Controller stops wakeup due to a detected collision during wakeup pattern transmission by receiving a valid Header on either channel.
100 COLLISION_WUP. Set when the Communication Controller stops wakeup due to a detected collision during wakeup pattern transmission by receiving a valid wakeup pattern on the configured wakeup channel.
101 COLLISION_UNKNOWN. Set when the Communication Controller stops wakeup by leaving "WAKEUP_DETECT" state after expiration of the wakeup timer without receiving a valid wakeup pattern or a valid Frame Header.
110 TRANSMITTED. Set when the Communication Controller has successfully completed the transmission of the wakeup pattern.
111 Reserved

PSL 6 24 - 29 rh 0x3f000000 POC Status Log

This may be combined with CHI command SEND_MTS. If both bits MTSA and MTSB are set to 1 an MTS symbol will be transmitted on both channels when requested by writing SUCC1.CMD=1000B.

Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
FDB 8 0 - 7 rw 0x000000ff First Dynamic Buffer
00 No group of Message Buffers exclusively for the static segment configured
01 ...7FH Message Buffers 0 to FDB-1 reserved for static segment
80 ...FF No dynamic Message Buffers configured

00 ...7EH Message Buffers from FFB to LCB assigned to the FIFO
7F All Message Buffers assigned to the FIFO
80 ...FF No Message Buffers assigned to the FIFO
LCB 8 16 - 23 rw 0x00ff0000 Last Configured Buffer
01 ...7FH Number of Message Buffers is LCB + 1
80 ...FFH No Message Buffer configured
SEC 2 24 - 25 rw 0x03000000
00 Reconfiguration of Message Buffers enabled with numbers < FFB enabled.
01 Reconfiguration of Message Buffers with numbers < FDB and with numbers >= FFB locked and transmission of Message Buffers for static segment with numbers >= FDB disabled
10 Reconfiguration of all Message Buffers locked
11 Reconfiguration of all Message Buffers locked and transmission of Message Buffers for static segment with numbers >= FDB disabled
SPLM 1 26 - 26 rw 0x04000000
0 Only Message Buffer 0 locked against reconfiguration
1 Both Message Buffers 0 and 1 are locked against reconfiguration

"Output Buffer Command Mask"

AddressERAY_OBCM_ADDR = 0xF0010710
Absolute addressableNo
Reset value0x00000000
C typeERAY_OBCM_t

ERAY_OBCM.bits "Output Buffer Command Mask"
Mask:ERAY_OBCM_MASK = 0x00030003
Masks:  ERAY_OBCM_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:ERAY_OBCM_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
RHSS 1 0 - 0 rwh 0x00000001 Read Header Section Shadow
0 Header Section is not read
1 Header Section selected for transfer from Message RAM to Output Buffer
RDSS 1 1 - 1 rwh 0x00000002 Read Data Section Shadow
0 Data Section is not read
1 Data Section selected for transfer from Message RAM to Output Buffer
RHSH 1 16 - 16 rh 0x00010000 Read Header Section Host
0 Header Section is not read
1 Header Section selected for transfer from Message RAM to Output Buffer
RDSH 1 17 - 17 rh 0x00020000 Read Data Section Host
0 Data Section is not read
1 Data Section selected for transfer from Message RAM to Output Buffer
 readable0x00030003 
writeable0x00000003
volatile0x00030003

ERAY_OBCR

"Output Buffer Command Request"

AddressERAY_OBCR_ADDR = 0xF0010714
Absolute addressableNo
Reset value0x00000000
C typeERAY_OBCR_t

ERAY_OBCR.bits "Output Buffer Command Request"
Mask:ERAY_OBCR_MASK = 0x007f837f
Masks:  ERAY_OBCR_<Bit field>_MASK
LSBs:ERAY_OBCR_<Bit field>_SHIFT
Bit field #Bits Bits' position Access Mask Description
OBRS 7 0 - 6 rw 0x0000007f Output Buffer Request Shadow
VIEW 1 8 - 8 rw 0x00000100 View Shadow Buffer
0 No action
1 Swap OBF Shadow and OBF Host
REQ 1 9 - 9 rw 0x00000200 Request Message RAM Transfer
0 No request
1 Transfer to OBF Shadow requested
OBSYS 1 15 - 15 rh 0x00008000 Output Buffer Busy Shadow
0 No transfer in progress
1 Transfer between Message RAM and OBF Shadow in progress
OBRH 7 16 - 22 rh 0x007f0000 Output Buffer Request Host
 readable0x007f837f 
writeable0x0000037f
volatile0x007f8000
